Please see coorection and verifications below:  
  

> [Quoting JoshDance](/thread/post/1433672#post1433672 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> I've taken the newest entry criteria from TeamAphid and consolidated it into the following... TeamAphid, please check these for validity:  
>    
>  ==============================================  
>  SCv1 = Repainting version of indicator (the one on the price)  
>  SCv2 = Non-repainting version of indicator (the one in the separate window)  
>    
>  Long entry:  
>    
>  In all cases, the previous bar close must be below the aqua line + 10 pips. If you enter with limit order to match the SCv1 entry. If you enter with Trend Power indicator, then we are not interested in previous bar obviously, only the bar where it is blue on SCv2 AND TP indicator is >= 0.14.   
>    
>  Wait for a blue bar on SCv2.  
>    
>  (1) If the corresponding bar on SCv1 is the first blue bar, or if the TrendPower indicator is >= 0.14, (or both, obviously), enter long now. Entry is done. Correct.  
>    
>  (2) Else, if there are prior blue bars on SCv1 and the TrendPower indicator is < 0.14, place a buy limit order at the closing price of the first blue bar on SCv1. Correct.  
>    
>  Check the charts at the next bar close.  
>  -If this closed bar caused the buy limit order to get filled, our entry is done.  
>  -If the buy limit is still open, and if TrendPower is >= 0.14, enter long (and obviously, cancel the buy limit order)—entry done. Else, wait until next bar close and recheck. Correct.  
>    
>  Obviously, if a non-blue-shaded bar appears, we abort our entry. Assume we placed our limit order and TrendPower is under 0.14. If a non-blue-shaded bar appears, then we check if first Take Profit level is hit. If it is hit, then we abort our entry, if not, we still wait for our entrly limit order to be filled, no matter what the colours of the bars are in between (obviously not red).   
>  ================================================
>

  * [#251](/thread/post/1434128#post1434128 "Post Permalink")

  * May 7, 2007 12:07pm  May 7, 2007 12:07pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

EXIT RULES - SL and TPs:  
  
Assume we are LONG 4 lots.  
  
1- If the entry is between yellow and green atr lines, then SL for all lots will be a close below yellow atr line.  
  
2- If entry is below yellow atr line, then SL will be bar colour change to red (there was no such a case during backtesting, we mean if entry is below yellow atr line, all trades closed in positive, gained big pips).  
  
3- If entry is between green and aqua atr lines, then SL will be touch of green atr line (this rule considerably reduced big losses and drawdowns, though caused only a few trades missing).  
  
4- First lot take profit (TP) - close between aqua and dodger blue atr lines.  
  
Exception 1- If entry is below green atr line, then do not wait for a close between green and aqua atr lines, exit the first lot when the price  
touches aqua atr line.  
  
Exception 2- If entry is within 10 pips of aqua atr line (bothsides), then   
exit the first lot when price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
5- Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
6- Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
7- Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
8-After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line. Same is applicable if first and and second lots are exited at profit and price touches back to green atr line.  
  
9- We are not using reentry strategy during the same cycle (during the same uptrend or downtrend).

The reason you have better win/loss ratio is you are bringing remaining lots immediately to BE after first TP together with very wide stoploss you use. We also use similar strategy (even tighter one, because we are not waiting for first TP to be filled and we define our SL as green atr line immediately), but we think this strategy makes the difference (reduces losses and drawdowns and improves profit factor considerably). 4.89:1 profit factor is incredible, in our opinion.

TeamAphid, regarding the new rules. I'm making a matrix of how to handle stops/exits/tp's, and I have a couple of questions:  
  
1) Does a red bar take precedence over all other exit/TP rules? IE, if in a long trade and a bar suddenly turns red, we take all profits/losses and exit all positions?  
  
2) When you say that a SL is at the green ATR line, do you mean that the stop will trail up and not move back down, or that the stop needs to move up AND down with the green line?  
  
In Rule #8, you say:

> Quote
> 
> Disliked
> 
> 8-After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line. (Does this mean that the SL's trail? I assume so.) Same is applicable if first and and second lots are exited at profit and price touches back to green atr line. (Could you explain what you mean here?)

  
3) For rule #7, you specify TP for lot #4, but in actuality, we just trail the SL along the green line and let it hit, right? So we never manually TP on lot #4, correct?  
  
Thanks for any clarifications you can provide--when I get my rule matrix finished later tonight, I'll post it and you guys, if you don't mind, can offer any corrections to it. I'm trying to get the rules in a fairly 'dummy-proof' format--my brain will overload if I have to think too much every 4 hours hehe :-)

  * May 8, 2007 7:26am  May 8, 2007 7:26am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

Please see answers below:  
  

> [Quoting JoshDance](/thread/post/1434842#post1434842 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> TeamAphid, regarding the new rules. I'm making a matrix of how to handle stops/exits/tp's, and I have a couple of questions:  
>    
>  1) Does a red bar take precedence over all other exit/TP rules? IE, if in a long trade and a bar suddenly turns red, we take all profits/losses and exit all positions? Yes, and if it is above yellow atr line -10 pips, then go short.  
>    
>  2) When you say that a SL is at the green ATR line, do you mean that the stop will trail up and not move back down, or that the stop needs to move up AND down with the green line? Stop can move up and down, whenever price touches green atr line, then exit.  
>    
>  In Rule #8, you say:  
>    
>  3) For rule #7, you specify TP for lot #4, but in actuality, we just trail the SL along the green line and let it hit, right? Right. So we never manually TP on lot #4, correct? No.  
>    
>  Thanks for any clarifications you can provide--when I get my rule matrix finished later tonight, I'll post it and you guys, if you don't mind, can offer any corrections to it. I'm trying to get the rules in a fairly 'dummy-proof' format--my brain will overload if I have to think too much every 4 hours hehe :-)
> 
> Ignored

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#266](/thread/post/1435061#post1435061 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited May 9, 2007 7:12am  May 8, 2007 1:57pm | Edited May 9, 2007 7:12am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

In practice, if a blue bar closes just a few pips above the green line, for a currency like GBPJPY, it is almost certain that you will be stopped out. Therefore, we think every trader should put a safety margin before using this rule. So, we agree with you about modifying this rule.  
  
Another recommendation could be if you are stopped out at green atr line and then if you see a close BELOW green atr line, then you can reenter although we are not using reentering strategy normally. By doing so, you will have a second chance with much better risk reward ratio. Please see attached chart for such a case.

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#269](/thread/post/1435894#post1435894 "Post Permalink")

  * May 9, 2007 7:34am  May 9, 2007 7:34am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

Because we did not want to limit traders by saying "if entry is below green atr +50 or +30, then SL will be below yellow line". There were only a couple cases in backtest period which had very close entry to green atr line and we did not take those trades. Therefore, for this rule, every trader should put a safety margin between green atr line and entry price according to their risk profile and apply green atr line stop. If entry is below that margin, then use "a close below yellow atr line" stop.   
  

> [Quoting billbss](/thread/post/1435742#post1435742 "View Quoted Post")

> Why do the rules allow such an entry if its almost certain to get stopped out?

  * [#272](/thread/post/1438320#post1438320 "Post Permalink")

  * May 11, 2007 10:39am  May 11, 2007 10:39am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

If you mean either 7/5 04:00 or 9/5 08:00 bars, they don't qualify as long trades since we are not entering in the middle of a cycle. For us, the cycle began at 27/4 08:00 bar (although it is repainting bar, we take that into consideration) and since the price was above aqua + 10 pips at the close of 12:00, we passed that trade. For such cases, we are waiting for a red bar to go short. We are not taking long signals in between.

What defines a cycle?  
What begins and ends a cycle? 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#274](/thread/post/1438376#post1438376 "Post Permalink")

  * May 11, 2007 12:34pm  May 11, 2007 12:34pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

Since we are not using reentry strategy as in the original pabloski rules, cycles starts when you get a signal in opposite direction of the previous signal. It does not matter if that signal is qualified to take the trade or not. For example, the cycle started on 27/4 08:00 bar, though we did pass this trade as we saw the beginning of cycle at the end of the next bar due to repainting issue of SC and it was above aqua +10 pips. Then cycle continues until we see a red bar (10/5 12:00 bar, sell signal) (does not matter if you are in the trade or not), therefore we are not taking any trades in between.  
  
Look at 19/4 04:00 bar where the cycle started. We were stoppped out on 19/4 16:00 bar according to grean atr exit rule and then we passed next short signal (23/4 04:00 bar), because cycle started and ended with stop-out. So cycles ends with stop-out or in other terms, exiting all lots with either profit or loss. Then next cycle should start with opposite trade direction, in this case 27/4 08:00 blue bar.  
  
  
  

> [Quoting billbss](/thread/post/1438358#post1438358 "View Quoted Post")

  * May 11, 2007 1:16pm  May 11, 2007 1:16pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar35717_6.gif) JoshDance](joshdance)

  * | Joined Mar 2007  | Status: Trader | [606 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=35717)

By my count, the last "good" trade to enter was 29/3 16:00. This was a blue bar, and it fit all the criteria. The 19/4 04:00 bar was not a good idea to enter although it fit the criteria, because it was nothing more than a higher low in a strong uptrend. Patience would have paid off in not taking that trade. Just not a good idea.  
  
Now, however, we've been in a bit of a consolidation phase for the last several weeks, and hopefully new trending will start soon. As has been said before, this system works well in trending markets, but not so well in ranging ones. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#276](/thread/post/1438427#post1438427 "Post Permalink")

  * May 11, 2007 2:07pm  May 11, 2007 2:07pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

You cannot enter on 29/3 16:00 bar, because you see that blue bar at the close of 20:00 bar due to repainting issue. If you use non-repainting SC ONLY to enter (not our 3 different entry methods), then you can enter at the open of 30/3 00:00 bar which is 231.73 (we don't take spread into consideration). Now the question is what will be your stoploss? If you use green atr line, then you were stopped out at the same bar. If you use original pabloski stop rules, will you be able to withstand 119 pips x 4 = 476 pips drawdown? And if you use original strategy, then our backtests showed that drawdown is much higher and profit is less. We are just trying to understand how you will trade mechanically this system.   
  
The same is true for 19/4 04:00 bar. How do you know this bar was not the end of uptrend when it closed? Then you shouldn't take short trade on 12/3 12:00 bar with the same approach. What we mean here if you use discretion to take trades, we believe you will end up with a completely different system and/or results. That is the danger of using discretion in mechanical systems. If entry/exit or stoploss fits all the criteria, then one should take the trade if the system will be traded 100% mechanically.  
  
We have integrated green atr stop and not reentry strategies to minimise losses in ranging markets and as a result we got very high profit factor with very reasonable drawdown for such a volatile currency.

  * [#289](/thread/post/1444267#post1444267 "Post Permalink")

  * May 18, 2007 9:22am  May 18, 2007 9:22am

But instead of using our 3 entry rules (limit orders, trend power entry etc.), if you use the new non-repainting indicator for entry (BUY when the bar is blue AND the close is below aqua atr +10 or vice versa), you will get 465 pips less compared to our entry rules, it is not actually a big deal.

  * [#305](/thread/post/1450455#post1450455 "Post Permalink")

  * May 25, 2007 11:59am  May 25, 2007 11:59am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

We are not using repainting indicator.  
  
Entry 1 looks at it, if they both match, then we enter, this means entry depends on non-repainting SC here. Because non-repainting SC lags, we use this entry after confirming the blue bar on non-repainting SC.  
  
Entry 2 looks at it to determine entry level, but after we see repainted blue bar. When do we look at it? After we see blue bar on non-repainting SC.  
  
Entry 3 happens after Entry 2 case is realised.  
  
As you can see, we base our entry criteria on non-repainting SC. Without confirming blue bar on non-repainting SC, we take no action and our backtests results are reliable and correct.

  * [#306](/thread/post/1450465#post1450465 "Post Permalink")

  * May 25, 2007 12:19pm  May 25, 2007 12:19pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

Sorry for confusion. We didn't say there was a 6000 pips difference __if you use repainting one's result using original pabloski rules.__   
  
As you know, we have started to post entry rules by using repainting indicator previously (at that time we hadn't observed live the indicator repainted itself on GBPJPY) and then when we observed it really repainted itself, we posted an important notice saying we were not using this indicator.  
When we started posting those entry rules, we had finished backtesting with repainting SC and the results were plus 22000 something pips. After repainting issue was fixed we tried to match entry rules which we used for repainting one by using non-repainting SC to decrease 6000 pips difference between __our backtest results with our modified rules using ONLY repainting SC and our backtest results with our modifed rules using non-repainting SC (current rules).__  
  
Original pabloski rules will produce totally different results with both repainting and non-repainting SC which will have bigger drawdowns and less pips.

  * [#311](/thread/post/1451371#post1451371 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 3:42pm  May 26, 2007 3:12pm | Edited 3:42pm 

  * [ zalakinc](zalakinc)

  * | Joined Dec 2005  | Status: Trader | [192 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4817)

Ok....here are the Teamaphid/Joshdance rules...A simplified version. Its actually longer than Teamaphid's version but its very simple in a sense that I divided all the rules into 8 sections. section 1-4 are for long...and section 5-8 are for short. I have used Joshdance's entry rules and Team aphid's exit and SL rules. when you see a red or blue bar forming...quickly go to the section that applies to that situation and thats the only section you need to refer to. Teamaphid, Please feel free to make any modifications you see necessary. I can also post this into word format if anybody wants.   
  
  
  
ATR Legend  
1st one from top: Blue  
2nd one: dodgeblue  
3rd: Aqua  
4th: green  
5th: yellow  
6rh: orange  
7th: red  
  
  
  
ENTRY:  
  
LONG ENTRY On the first Blue bar AND the close is below aqua atr +10   
  
SHORT ENTRY/SELL: Closed Bar is Red and above yellow-10   
  
Pasted from <[http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...=23592&page=17](http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=23592&page=17)>   
  
  
9- We are not using reentry strategy during the same cycle (during the same uptrend or downtrend).  
cycles starts when you get a signal in opposite direction of the previous signal. It does not matter if that signal is qualified to take the trade or not  
  
**EXIT RULES - SL and TPs:**  
  
  
  
RULE SET 1: IF LONG ENTRY IS BELOW YELLOW LINE   
  
-> Stop loss will be bar color change to red(there was no such a case during backtesting, we mean if entry is below yellow atr line, all trades closed in positive, gained big pips).  
  
First Lot exit: the first lot when the price touches aqua atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
RULE SET 2: IF LONG ENTRY BETWEEN YELLOW AND GREEN LINE  
  
-> Initial stop loss will be close below Yellow ATR Line/But a Red bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
Exit the first lot when the price touches aqua atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
RULE SET 3 IF LONG ENTRY BETWEEN GREEN AND AQUA LINE  
  
SL will be touch of green ATR Line/But a Red bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
First lot: close between aqua and dodger blue atr lines  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
In practice, if a blue bar closes just a few pips above the green line, for a currency like GBPJPY, it is almost certain that you will be stopped out. Therefore, we think every trader should put a safety margin before using this rule. So, we agree with you about modifying this rule.  
Another recommendation could be if you are stopped out at green atr line and then if you see a close BELOW green atr line, then you can reenter although we are not using reentering strategy normally. By doing so, you will have a second chance with much better risk reward ratio. Please see attached chart for such a case.  
  
RULE SET 4: IF LONG ENTRY BETWEEN AQUA AND +10 LINE  
  
exit the first lot when price touches dodger blue atr line/But a Red bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line. Same is applicable if first and and second lots are exited at profit and price touches back to green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
  
RULE SET 5: IF SHORT ENTRY IS ABOVE AQUA LINE - all positions will be exited if bars turn to BLUE  
  
-> FOR SHORT STOP LOSS WILL BE BAR COLOR CHANGE TO BLUE  
  
exit the first lot when the price touches YELLOW atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
  
RULE SET 6: IF SHORT ENTRY BETWEEN AQUA AND GREEN LINE  
  
-> Initial stop loss will be close ABOW AQUA ATR Line/But a Blue bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
Exit the first lot when the price touches Yellow atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
RULE SET 7 SHORT ENTRY BETWEEN GREEN AND YELLOW LINE  
  
SL will be touch of green ATR Line/But a Blue bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
First lot: close between Yellow and Orange atr lines  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
In practice, if a red bar closes just a few pips BELOW the green line, for a currency like GBPJPY, it is almost certain that you will be stopped out. Therefore, we think every trader should put a safety margin before using this rule. So, we agree with you about modifying this rule.  
Another recommendation could be if you are stopped out at green atr line and then if you see a close above green atr line, then you can reenter although we are not using reentering strategy normally. By doing so, you will have a second chance with much better risk reward ratio.   
  
RULE SET 8 IF SHORT ENTRY BETWEEN AQUA AND +10 LINE OR YELLOW -10  
  
exit the first lot when price touches Orange ATR Line/But a Blue bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
  
______________________________________________________________________

  * [#313](/thread/post/1451987#post1451987 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 8:08pm  May 28, 2007 8:10am | Edited 8:08pm 

  * [ zalakinc](zalakinc)

  * | Joined Dec 2005  | Status: Trader | [192 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=4817)

Ok....here are the Teamaphid/Joshdance rules...A simplified version. Its actually longer than Teamaphid's version but its very simple in a sense that I divided all the rules into 8 sections. section 1-4 are for long...and section 5-8 are for short. I have used Joshdance's entry rules and Team aphid's exit and SL rules. when you see a red or blue bar forming...quickly go to the section that applies to that situation and thats the only section you need to refer to. Teamaphid, Please feel free to make any modifications you see necessary. I can also post this into word format if anybody wants.   
  
  
  
ATR Legend  
1st one from top: Blue  
2nd one: dodgeblue  
3rd: Aqua  
4th: green  
5th: yellow  
6rh: orange  
7th: red  
  
  
  
ENTRY:  
  
LONG ENTRY On the first Blue bar AND the close is below aqua atr +10   
  
SHORT ENTRY/SELL: Closed Bar is Red and above yellow-10   
  
Pasted from <[http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...=23592&page=17](http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=23592&page=17)>   
  
  
9- We are not using reentry strategy during the same cycle (during the same uptrend or downtrend).  
cycles starts when you get a signal in opposite direction of the previous signal. It does not matter if that signal is qualified to take the trade or not  
  
**EXIT RULES - SL and TPs:**  
  
  
  
RULE SET 1: IF LONG ENTRY IS BELOW YELLOW LINE   
  
-> Stop loss will be bar color change to red(there was no such a case during backtesting, we mean if entry is below yellow atr line, all trades closed in positive, gained big pips).  
  
First Lot exit: the first lot when the price touches aqua atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
RULE SET 2: IF LONG ENTRY BETWEEN YELLOW AND GREEN LINE  
  
-> Initial stop loss will be close below Yellow ATR Line/But a Red bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
Exit the first lot when the price touches aqua atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
RULE SET 3 IF LONG ENTRY BETWEEN GREEN AND AQUA LINE  
  
SL will be touch of green ATR Line/But a Red bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
First lot: close between aqua and dodger blue atr lines  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
In practice, if a blue bar closes just a few pips above the green line, for a currency like GBPJPY, it is almost certain that you will be stopped out. Therefore, we think every trader should put a safety margin before using this rule. So, we agree with you about modifying this rule.  
Another recommendation could be if you are stopped out at green atr line and then if you see a close BELOW green atr line, then you can reenter although we are not using reentering strategy normally. By doing so, you will have a second chance with much better risk reward ratio. Please see attached chart for such a case.  
  
RULE SET 4: IF LONG ENTRY BETWEEN AQUA AND +10 LINE  
  
exit the first lot when price touches dodger blue atr line/But a Red bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line. Same is applicable if first and and second lots are exited at profit and price touches back to green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - when the price touches dodger blue atr line.  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches blue atr line.  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot.  
  
  
RULE SET 5: IF SHORT ENTRY IS ABOVE AQUA LINE - all positions will be exited if bars turn to BLUE  
  
-> FOR SHORT STOP LOSS WILL BE BAR COLOR CHANGE TO BLUE  
  
exit the first lot when the price touches YELLOW atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
  
RULE SET 6: IF SHORT ENTRY BETWEEN AQUA AND GREEN LINE  
  
-> Initial stop loss will be close ABOW AQUA ATR Line/But a Blue bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
Exit the first lot when the price touches Yellow atr line.  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
RULE SET 7 SHORT ENTRY BETWEEN GREEN AND YELLOW LINE  
  
SL will be touch of green ATR Line/But a Blue bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
First lot: close between Yellow and Orange atr lines  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot  
  
In practice, if a red bar closes just a few pips BELOW the green line, for a currency like GBPJPY, it is almost certain that you will be stopped out. Therefore, we think every trader should put a safety margin before using this rule. So, we agree with you about modifying this rule.  
Another recommendation could be if you are stopped out at green atr line and then if you see a close above green atr line, then you can reenter although we are not using reentering strategy normally. By doing so, you will have a second chance with much better risk reward ratio.   
  
RULE SET 8 IF SHORT ENTRY BETWEEN YELLOW and -10  
  
exit the first lot when price touches Orange ATR Line/But a Blue bar takes Precedence over any other stop loss  
  
After exiting first lot, SL for all remaining lots will be touch of green atr line.  
  
Second lot TP - touches ORANGE ATR LINE  
  
Third lot TP - when the price touches RED ATR LINE  
  
Fourth lot TP - After exiting 3rd lot with profit, trail the fourth lot with green atr line, whenever price touches green atr line, exit the fourth lot

The recent long is valid and it is not on the same cycle since a red bar appeared previously. We are not looking for a red bar to be a valid short entry, as long as it appears, we accept a new cycle begins. Therefore recent long entry is valid as it comes after a red bar cycle.

hi bhatiaashish007,  
  
this is a Windows issue. Just right clicks on your file and choose rename, then delete the uneeded caracters. You should have the indicator name like this: StepChoppyBars_v2.mq4 for version 2  
  
Same thing for the indicator if you want to use it : StepChoppy_v2.mq4  
  
Hapy trading,

> [Quoting TeamAphid](/thread/post/1434128#post1434128 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> EXIT RULES - SL and TPs:  
>    
>  4- First lot take profit (TP) - close between aqua and dodger blue atr lines.  
>    
>  Exception 1- If entry is below green atr line, then do not wait for a close between green and aqua atr lines, exit the first lot when the price  
>  touches aqua atr line.

> 
> Ignored

And looking back on the previous winning Long trade entered on 2007.06.12 at 240.33 (attached), by using the Aphid rules and entering on a Limit order you entered below the green line, giving more room for the trade to move as the SL was the yellow atr line (red arrow in pic). However if you were to use just StepChoppyV2 and trade without discretion (ie no re-entries) then you would have been stopped out of this trade and missed the big run?  
  
I like the simplicity of JoshDance's suggestion of trading just StepChoppyv2, however the extra pips on trades like this will be hard to leave behind. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

  * [#393](/thread/post/1493526#post1493526 "Post Permalink")

  * Jul 13, 2007 11:07am  Jul 13, 2007 11:07am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar17832_4.gif) TeamAphid](teamaphid)

  * | Joined Sep 2006  | Status: Team Work!!!! | [302 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=17832)

This is correct and you should be long as our limit buy order was hit on 12/7 08:00 bar. At that time, the green ATR line was at 247.68 which was too close as the low of the same bar was at 247.69. Therefore, you could put your SL below yellow ATR line to give room, but now we are well above green ATR line (247.86). If you don't want any risk and lock some profits, you can use green ATR line as your SL. If you love risk and give the trade more room, then you can keep your SL below yellow ATR line.

  * | Joined Nov 2006  | Status: Trader | [159 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=24144)

Hi Pabloski!  
  
Welcome back and thanks for sharing your method. I have just been following on demo, not live trading but there has been some very nice trades the last couple of months as a result of the carry unwind and subsequent bounce back.  
  
I had a question for anyone following this system using the modified Aphid rules. The 29.08.2007 16:00 candle (Alpari Ru) signalled a long limit order entry as TrendPower was below 0.14. However by the close the following candle (20:00) TrendPower was greater than 0.14 which indicates to take the entry at this point. The one thing to note though was that by this time price was above the Aqua Line (+10 points) by ~45pips. So would this trade have now been disregarded or because it hadn't yet reached TP1 then still take the entry?  
  
While only demoing this method still, I took the trade and had the initial SL just below green line and also had it just below the low of the previous candle, ie the 16:00 candle. I was then fortunate enough to be sleeping when a couple of bars poked below the green line but did not hit my initial SL. So at the moment I still have all 4 lots on this trade open.  
  
So for those still following and using the modified rules, would be good to hear your take on this entry?  
  
Thanks..
